#rework
TUR_remove_add_dynamic_modifiers = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_national_economy } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_national_economy }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_national_economy }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_agrarian_economy } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_agrarian_economy }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_agrarian_economy }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_second_constitutional_era } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_second_constitutional_era }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_second_constitutional_era }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_army_of_a_bygone_era } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_army_of_a_bygone_era }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_army_of_a_bygone_era }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_army_of_the_modern_era } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_army_of_the_modern_era }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_army_of_the_modern_era }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_donanma_yi_humayun } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_donanma_yi_humayun }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_donanma_yi_humayun }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_havacilik_komisyonu } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_havacilik_komisyonu }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_havacilik_komisyonu }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_sublime_realm } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_sublime_realm }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_sublime_realm }
		}
	}
}

TUR_add_appropriate_grand_vizier_for_bop = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_mahmud_sevket } }
			set_power_balance = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				right_side = TUR_government_committee_struggle_mahmud_sevket
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_said_halim } }
			set_power_balance = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				right_side = TUR_government_committee_struggle_said_halim
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_nazim_pasha } }
			set_power_balance = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				right_side = TUR_government_committee_struggle_nazim_pasha
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_ibrahim_hakki } }
			set_power_balance = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				right_side = TUR_government_committee_struggle_ibrahim_hakki
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_ali_fuat_turkgeldi } }
			set_power_balance = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				right_side = TUR_government_committee_struggle_ali_fuat_turkgeldi
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_ahmet_riza } }
			set_power_balance = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				right_side = TUR_government_committee_struggle_ahmet_riza
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_huseyin_hilmi_pasha } }
			set_power_balance = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				right_side = TUR_government_committee_struggle_huseyin_hilmi_pasha
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_ahmet_izzet } }
			set_power_balance = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				right_side = TUR_government_committee_struggle_ahmet_izzet
			}
		}
	}
}

TUR_remove_current_sultan = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = HJZ_hussein_bin_ali }
		remove_ideas = HJZ_hussein_bin_ali
		set_country_flag = TUR_had_HJZ_hussein_bin_ali
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_mehmed_V }
		remove_ideas = TUR_mehmed_V
		set_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_mehmed_V
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_yusuf_izzettin }
		remove_ideas = TUR_yusuf_izzettin
		set_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_yusuf_izzettin
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_mehmed_VI }
		remove_ideas = TUR_mehmed_VI
		set_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_mehmed_VI
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_abdulmecid_II }
		remove_ideas = TUR_abdulmecid_II
		set_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_abdulmecid_II
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_ahmed_nihad }
		remove_ideas = TUR_ahmed_nihad
		set_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_ahmed_nihad
	}
}

TUR_add_current_sultan = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_had_HJZ_hussein_bin_ali }
		add_ideas = HJZ_hussein_bin_ali
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_mehmed_V }
		add_ideas = TUR_mehmed_V
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_yusuf_izzettin }
		add_ideas = TUR_yusuf_izzettin
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_mehmed_VI }
		add_ideas = TUR_mehmed_VI
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_abdulmecid_II }
		add_ideas = TUR_abdulmecid_II
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_ahmed_nihad }
		add_ideas = TUR_ahmed_nihad
	}
	clr_country_flag = TUR_had_HJZ_hussein_bin_ali
	clr_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_mehmed_V
	clr_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_yusuf_izzettin
	clr_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_mehmed_VI
	clr_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_abdulmecid_II
	clr_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_ahmed_nihad
}

TUR_promote_officers_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_character = TUR_suleyman_faik
			TUR_suleyman_faik = { is_unit_leader = no } #1.1.1913
		}
		add_corps_commander_role = {
			character = TUR_suleyman_faik
			traits = { trait_engineer cavalry_leader career_officer }
			skill = 2
			attack_skill = 1
			defense_skill = 2
			planning_skill = 3
			logistics_skill = 2
		}
		TUR_suleyman_faik = { set_character_name = TUR_suleyman_faik_pasha }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_character = TUR_hasan_riza
			TUR_hasan_riza = { is_unit_leader = no } #30.2.1914
		}
		add_corps_commander_role = {
			character = TUR_hasan_riza
			traits = { war_hero cavalry_leader harsh_leader career_officer }
			skill = 3
			attack_skill = 1
			defense_skill = 3
			planning_skill = 3
			logistics_skill = 2
		}
		TUR_hasan_riza = { set_character_name = TUR_hasan_riza_pasha }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_character = TUR_cevat_cobanli
			TUR_cevat_cobanli = { is_unit_leader = no } #29.11.1914
		}
		add_corps_commander_role = {
			character = TUR_cevat_cobanli
			traits = { inflexible_strategist desert_fox old_guard }
			skill = 3
			attack_skill = 2
			defense_skill = 3

TUR_domestic_weapon_research_tank = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_council_of_military_scientific_research
				has_completed_focus = TRS_domestic_weapon_companies
			}
			has_idea = tulomsas
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = TRS
				check_variable = { TUR_aoabe_army_attack_factor < 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_aoabe_army_defence_factor < 0 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TRS_domestic_weapon_research_tt
			add_to_variable = { TUR_o4a_army_attack_factor = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_o4a_army_attack_factor = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_o4a_army_attack_factor_tt = -0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_o4a_army_attack_factor_tt = -0.005 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = TRS }
				check_variable = { TUR_aoabe_army_attack_factor < 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_aoabe_army_defence_factor < 0 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_domestic_weapon_research_tt
			add_to_variable = { TUR_aoabe_army_attack_factor = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_aoabe_army_defence_factor = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_aoabe_army_attack_factor_tt = -0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_aoabe_army_defence_factor_tt = -0.005 }
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

TUR_debt_value_check = {
    hidden_effect = {
		set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_1 = 0 }
		set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_1_opposite = 0 }
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods < 0 } }
			set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_1 = -0.01 }
			set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_1_opposite = 0.01 }
			ROOT = { add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_1 = -0.01 } }
			ROOT = { add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_1_opposite = 0.01 } }
		}
		set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2_1 = 0 }
		set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2_1_opposite = 0 }
		set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_2 = 0 }

TUR_remove_debt_1_ROOT = {
	TUR = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_1
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.01 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_current_amount_ROOT
			}
			add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = 0.01 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = opda_consumer_goods
				min = 0
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { ROOT = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods } }
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.01 } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_current_amount_ROOT
		}
		else = { custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_1_ROOT }
		hidden_effect = {
			ROOT = {
				add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = 0.01 }
				add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = -0.01 }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = opda_consumer_goods
					max = 0
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					var = opda_consumer_goods_opposite
					min = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_debt_value_check = yes
}

TUR_remove_debt_5_ROOT = {
	TUR = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_5
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.05 } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_current_amount_ROOT
			}
			add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = -0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = 0.05 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = opda_consumer_goods
				min = 0
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { ROOT = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods } }
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.05 } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_current_amount_ROOT
		}
		else = { custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_5_ROOT }
		hidden_effect = {
			ROOT = {
				add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = 0.05 }
				add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = -0.05 }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = opda_consumer_goods
					max = 0
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					var = opda_consumer_goods_opposite
					min = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_debt_value_check = yes
}

					var = opda_consumer_goods_opposite
					min = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_debt_value_check = yes
}
TUR_remove_debt_85_BEL = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_85
		if = {
			limit = { BEL = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.85 } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_current_amount_BEL
		}
		add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = -0.85 }
		add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = 0.85 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = opda_consumer_goods
			min = 0
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = opda_consumer_goods_opposite
			max = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { BEL = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods } }
		if = {
			limit = { BEL = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.85 } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_current_amount_BEL
		}
		else = { custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_85_BEL }
		hidden_effect = {
			BEL = {
				add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = 0.85 }
				add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = -0.85 }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = opda_consumer_goods
					max = 0
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					var = opda_consumer_goods_opposite
					min = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_debt_value_check = yes
}

TUR_investment_add_effect = {
	effect_tooltip = {
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = FRA } }
			activate_mission = TUR_investments_from_FRA
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = ENG } }
			activate_mission = TUR_investments_from_ENG
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = GER } }
			activate_mission = TUR_investments_from_GER
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = BEL } }
			activate_mission = TUR_investments_from_BEL
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = HOL } }
			activate_mission = TUR_investments_from_HOL
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = ITA } }
			activate_mission = TUR_investments_from_ITA
		}

		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = USA } }
			activate_mission = TUR_investments_from_USA
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = RUS } }
			activate_mission = TUR_investments_from_RUS
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_investment_add_effect_tt
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_infrastructure } }
			var:FROM.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = FRA } }
				TUR_add_debt_5_FRA = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = ENG } }
				TUR_add_debt_5_ENG = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = GER } }
				TUR_add_debt_5_GER = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = BEL } }
				TUR_add_debt_5_BEL = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = HOL } }
				TUR_add_debt_5_HOL = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = ITA } }
				TUR_add_debt_5_ITA = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = AUS } }
				TUR_add_debt_5_AUS = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = RUS } }
				TUR_add_debt_5_RUS = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = USA } }
				TUR_add_debt_5_USA = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_consumer } }
			var:FROM.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			if = {

			}
			if = {

TUR_anatolian_grain_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain
			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_2 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_2
			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_3 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_3
			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_4 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_4
			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_5
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_5 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_5
			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_6
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_6 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_6
			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_7
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_7 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_7
			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_8
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_8 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_8
			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_9
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_9 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_9
			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_10
		}
	}
}

TUR_reduce_naval_blockade = {
	add_to_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade = -1 }
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 1 } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_naval_blockade_reduce_1
			add_to_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.01 }
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_ideas = TUR_naval_blockade
				add_ideas = TUR_naval_blockade
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade < 2 } }
			remove_ideas = TUR_naval_blockade
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { global.TUR_reduce_naval_blockade_naval_blockade = TUR_naval_blockade }
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_great_famine_of_syria }
				country_event = { id = ottoman.161 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_state_development_category = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = wasteland }
		set_state_category = pastoral
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = enclave }
		set_state_category = pastoral
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = tiny_island }
		set_state_category = small_island
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = pastoral }
		set_state_category = rural
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = small_island }
		set_state_category = rural
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = rural }
		set_state_category = town
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = town }
		set_state_category = large_town
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = large_town }
		set_state_category = city
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = city }
		set_state_category = large_city
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = large_city }
		set_state_category = metropolis
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = metropolis }
		set_state_category = megalopolis
	}
}

TUR_government_stability_calculate = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_government_stability_var > TUR_government_stability_max } }
			set_variable = { TUR_government_stability_var = TUR_government_stability_max }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_government_stability_var < 0 } }
			set_variable = { TUR_government_stability_var = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = TUR_unshaken_dignity
				check_variable = { TUR_government_stability_var < 50 }
			}
			country_event = { id = ottoman.1 hours = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = TUR_the_victorious
				check_variable = { TUR_government_stability_var < 50 }
			}
			country_event = { id = ottoman.9 hours = 2 }
		}
	}
}
TUR_government_popularity_calculate = {
	hidden_effect = {
		set_variable = { TUR_neutrality_popularity = party_popularity@neutrality }
		set_variable = { TUR_democratic_popularity = party_popularity@democratic }
		set_variable = { TUR_fascism_popularity = party_popularity@fascism }
		set_variable = { TUR_communism_popularity = party_popularity@communism }
		#
		set_variable = { TUR_po_neutrality_popularity = TUR_neutrality_popularity }
		divide_variable = { TUR_po_neutrality_popularity = 2 }
		set_variable = { TUR_po_democratic_popularity = TUR_democratic_popularity }
		divide_variable = { TUR_po_democratic_popularity = 2 }
		set_variable = { TUR_po_fascism_popularity = TUR_fascism_popularity }
		divide_variable = { TUR_po_fascism_popularity = 2 }
		set_variable = { TUR_po_communism_popularity = TUR_communism_popularity }
		divide_variable = { TUR_po_communism_popularity = 2 }
		#
		set_variable = { TUR_itf_popularity = 0 }
		set_variable = { TUR_po_itf_popularity = 0 }
		set_variable = { TUR_hif_popularity = 0 }
		set_variable = { TUR_po_hif_popularity = 0 }
		#
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_neutrality_itf }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_itf_popularity = TUR_neutrality_popularity }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_po_itf_popularity = TUR_po_neutrality_popularity }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_neutrality_hif }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_hif_popularity = TUR_neutrality_popularity }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_po_hif_popularity = TUR_po_neutrality_popularity }
		}
		#
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_democratic_itf }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_itf_popularity = TUR_democratic_popularity }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_po_itf_popularity = TUR_po_democratic_popularity }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_democratic_hif }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_hif_popularity = TUR_democratic_popularity }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_po_hif_popularity = TUR_po_democratic_popularity }
		}
		#
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_fascism_itf }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_itf_popularity = TUR_fascism_popularity }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_po_itf_popularity = TUR_po_fascism_popularity }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_fascism_hif }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_hif_popularity = TUR_fascism_popularity }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_po_hif_popularity = TUR_po_fascism_popularity }
		}
		#
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_communism_itf }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_itf_popularity = TUR_communism_popularity }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_po_itf_popularity = TUR_po_communism_popularity }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_communism_hif }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_hif_popularity = TUR_communism_popularity }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_po_hif_popularity = TUR_po_communism_popularity }
		}
		#############
		if = {
			limit = { TUR_regime_is_more_popular_than_opposition_twice = no }
			activate_mission = TUR_disruptive_opposition
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { TUR_regime_is_more_popular_than_opposition = no }
			activate_mission = TUR_paralyzing_opposition
		}
	}
}

TUR_depoliticize_army_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_depoliticize_army_effect_1
		hidden_effect = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_1
				add_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_2
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_2 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_depoliticize_army_effect_2
		hidden_effect = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_2
				add_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_3
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_3 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_depoliticize_army_effect_3
		hidden_effect = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_3
				add_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_4
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_4 }
		remove_ideas = TUR_army_factionalism_4
	}
	else = {
		add_command_power = 20
		add_to_variable = {
			tooltip = TUR_government_stability_add_5
			TUR_government_stability_var = 5
		}
	}
	TUR_government_stability_calculate = yes
}

			limit = { has_idea = TUR_crippling_illiteracy }
			remove_ideas = TUR_crippling_illiteracy
			add_ideas = TUR_crippling_illiteracy
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TUR_indoctrinated_education }
			remove_ideas = TUR_indoctrinated_education
			add_ideas = TUR_indoctrinated_education
		}
	}
}

TUR_liberation_war_defeat_effect = { #rework
	FROM = { white_peace = ROOT }
	if = {
		limit = {
			ENG = { has_country_flag = great_war_winner }
		}
		ENG = { puppet = TUR }
	}
	set_cosmetic_tag = TUR_Sultanate
	if = {
		limit = {
			GRE = { has_completed_focus = GRE_venizelos_tittoni_agreement }
			ITA = { has_country_flag = great_war_winner }
		}
		824 = { transfer_state_to = ITA }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			SOV = {
				exists = no
			}
			RUS = {
				exists = yes
				has_country_flag = great_war_winner
			}
		}
		RUS = {
			transfer_state = 352
			transfer_state = 353
			transfer_state = 806
		}
		else = {
			ARM = {
				transfer_state = 352
				transfer_state = 353
				transfer_state = 806
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			GRE = { has_country_flag = pontus_rebellion }
		}
		PON = {
			transfer_state = 354
			transfer_state = 1034
			transfer_state = 355
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					ARM = {
						owns_state = 353
					}
				}
				transfer_state = 354
				transfer_state = 1034
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			GRE = {
				has_country_flag = pontus_confederation
			}
			SOV = {
				exists = yes
			}
		}
		ARM = {
			annex_country = {
				target = PON
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = PON
				}
				remove_core_of = PON
				add_core_of = ARM
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = PONARM
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			FRA = { has_country_flag = great_war_winner }
		}
		TUR = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 344
						state = 857
						state = 829
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = FRA
			}					
		}
	}
	release = KUR
}

TUR_create_armenian_vilayet = {
	create_dynamic_country = {
		original_tag = ARM
		reserve_dynamic_country = yes
		set_country_flag = western_armenia
		set_country_flag = is_ottoman_autonomous_vilayet
		set_country_flag = has_adopted_TUR_minority_system
		hidden_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = ARM_vilayet
			set_stability = 62
			set_war_support = 54
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_create_armenian_vilayet_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = { remove_core_of = ARA }
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 353
						state = 1022
						state = 352
						state = 350
						state = 881
						state = 1025
						state = 349
						state = 1026
						state = 1024
						state = 1057
						state = 857
						state = 344
						state = 1033
						state = 348
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ARA
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						tag = TUR
						is_subject_of = TUR
					}
				}
				OR = {
					state = 353
					state = 1022
					state = 352
					state = 350
					state = 881
					state = 1025
					state = 349
					state = 1026
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = ottoman.151.b.tt
			hidden_effect = { transfer_state_to = ARA }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					state = 353
					state = 1022
					state = 352
					state = 350
					state = 881
					state = 1025
					state = 349
					state = 1026
				}
				check_variable = { TUR_armenian_state_level > 0 }
			}
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenian_minority }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 353
					state = 1022
					state = 352
					state = 350
					state = 881
					state = 1025
					state = 349
					state = 1026
				}
				check_variable = { TUR_turkish_state_level > 0 }
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_turkish_minority }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				elections_allowed = yes
				election_frequency = 48
			}
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 45
				neutrality = 40
				fascism = 7
				communism = 8
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = democratic
				name = ARA_democratic
				long_name = ARA_democratic_long
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				name = ARA_neutrality
				long_name = ARA_neutrality_long
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				name = ARA_fascism
				long_name = ARA_fascism_long
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = communism
				name = ARA_communism
				long_name = ARA_communism_long
			}
			ARM = {
				ARM_mekertich_portukalian = {
					set_nationality = ARA
					promote_character = liberal_conservatism
				}
			}
			load_focus_tree = empty_focus
			set_research_slots = 2
			set_capital = {
				state = 353
				remember_old_capital = no
			}
		}
		set_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_factor = -0.007 }
		set_variable = { TUR_greek_population_factor = -0.007 }
		set_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_factor = -0.007 }
		set_variable = { TUR_arab_population_factor = -0.007 }
		set_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_factor = -0.007 }
		set_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_factor = 0 }
		set_variable = { TUR_kurdish_population_factor = -0.007 }
		set_variable = { TUR_assyrian_population_factor = -0.007 }
		set_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_factor = -0.007 }
		set_variable = { TUR_turkish_population_factor = -0.007 }

		set_variable = { TUR_sunni_population_factor = -0.003 }
		set_variable = { TUR_orthodox_population_factor = -0.003 }
		set_variable = { TUR_apostolic_population_factor = 0.002 }
		set_variable = { TUR_judaic_population_factor = -0.003 }
		set_variable = { TUR_syriac_population_factor = -0.003 }
		set_variable = { TUR_shia_population_factor = -0.003 }
		set_variable = { TUR_catholic_population_factor = -0.003 }
		add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ARM_sublime_realm }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { TUR = { has_country_flag = TUR_millet_system_population_selected } }
				set_country_flag = TUR_millet_system_population_selected
				set_variable = { TUR_millet_system_population_button = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { TUR = { has_country_flag = TUR_millet_system_population_nationality_selected } }
				set_country_flag = TUR_millet_system_population_nationality_selected
				set_variable = { TUR_millet_system_population_nationality_button = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { TUR = { has_country_flag = TUR_millet_system_population_religion_selected } }
				set_country_flag = TUR_millet_system_population_religion_selected
				set_variable = { TUR_millet_system_population_religion_button = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { TUR = { has_country_flag = TUR_millet_system_onmap_selected } }
				set_country_flag = TUR_millet_system_onmap_selected
				set_variable = { TUR_millet_system_onmap_button = 2 }
			}
			if = {

				set_country_flag = TUR_millet_system_description_selected
				set_variable = { TUR_millet_system_description_button = 2 }
			}
			country_event = ottoman.133
		}
	}
	TUR = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = ottoman.151.b.tt2
		hidden_effect = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = ARA
				autonomous_state = autonomy_tgwr_ottoman_autonomous_vilayet

TUR_create_italian_libya_autonomy = {
	create_dynamic_country = {
		original_tag = LBA
		reserve_dynamic_country = yes
		set_country_flag = LBA_trablusgarp
		hidden_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = LBA_trablusgarp
			set_stability = 50
			set_war_support = 50
			every_state = { remove_core_of = TRB }
			every_state = {
				limit = { has_state_flag = TUR_trablusgarp }
				remove_core_of = FROM
				add_claim_by = FROM
				add_core_of = FROM
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						tag = FROM
						is_subject_of = FROM
					}
				}
				has_state_flag = TUR_trablusgarp
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = ww1_italianturkish.16.a.tt
			hidden_effect = { transfer_state_to = TRB }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 15
				neutrality = 65
				fascism = 20
				communism = 0
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = democratic
				name = TRB_democratic
				long_name = TRB_democratic_long
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				name = TRB_neutrality
				long_name = TRB_neutrality_long
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				name = TRB_fascism
				long_name = TRB_fascism_long
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = communism
				name = TRB_communism
				long_name = TRB_communism_long
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = { has_character = TRP_sulayman_al_baruni }
				TRP_sulayman_al_baruni = {
					set_nationality = TRB
					promote_character = civilian_dictatorship
				}
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = { has_character = TRB_ferhat_efendi }
				TRB_ferhat_efendi = {
					set_nationality = TRB
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = { ideology = conservatism }
					}
				}
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = { has_character = TRB_yusuf_shetvan }
				TRB_yusuf_shetvan = {
					set_nationality = TRB
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = { ideology = reactionism }
					}
				}
			}
			load_focus_tree = empty_focus
			set_research_slots = 1
			set_capital = {
				state = 448
				remember_old_capital = no
			}
		}
	}
	ROOT = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = ww1_italianturkish.16.a.tt2
		hidden_effect = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = TRB
				autonomous_state = autonomy_puppet
				freedom_level = 0.3
			}
			country_event = ww1_italianturkish.20
		}
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					tag = FROM
					AND = {
						is_subject_of = FROM
						OR = {
							has_autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_ottoman_autonomous_vilayet
							has_autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_ottoman_committee_government
						}
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_state_flag = TUR_trablusgarp }
			is_core_of = LBA
		}
		transfer_state_to = LBA
	}
}

TUR_add_1_8th_of_population = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_variable = TUR_state_population_to_be_added }
		add_manpower = TUR_state_population_to_be_added
	}
	else = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { TUR_state_population_to_be_added = state_population }
			divide_variable = { TUR_state_population_to_be_added = 8 }
			add_manpower = TUR_state_population_to_be_added
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_state_population_to_be_added = state_population }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_state_population_to_be_added = 8 }
			add_manpower = TUR_state_population_to_be_added
		}
	}
}
TUR_remove_1_8th_of_population = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_variable = TUR_state_population_to_be_removed }
		add_manpower = TUR_state_population_to_be_removed
	}
	else = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { TUR_state_population_to_be_removed = state_population }
			divide_variable = { TUR_state_population_to_be_removed = -8 }
			add_manpower = TUR_state_population_to_be_removed
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_state_population_to_be_removed = state_population }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_state_population_to_be_removed = -8 }
			add_manpower = TUR_state_population_to_be_removed
		}
	}
}

GER_TUR_military_mission_effect = {
	TUR = {
		set_global_flag = GER_TUR_military_mission
		add_ideas = TUR_german_military_command
		custom_effect_tooltip = escape_line
		GER = {
			every_character = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_character = GER_colmar_von_der_goltz
						is_character = GER_otto_liman_von_sanders
						is_character = GER_fritz_bronsart_von_schellendorf
						is_character = GER_kress_von_kressenstein
						is_character = GER_wilhelm_souchon
						is_character = GER_guido_von_usedom
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_character = GER_colmar_von_der_goltz
					}
					set_character_name = TUR_colmar_von_der_goltz
					set_character_flag = unit_leader_can_die_from_sickness
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { is_character = GER_otto_liman_von_sanders }
					set_portraits = {
						army = {
							large = "gfx/leaders/TUR/TUR_liman_von_sanders.png"
							small = "gfx/interface/ideas/TUR/idea_TUR_liman_von_sanders.png"
						}
					}
				}
				set_nationality = TUR
			}
		}
	}
}
restraint_GER_TUR_military_mission_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_german_military_command_2 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_german_military_command_2
			add_idea = TUR_german_military_command
		}
	}	
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_german_military_command }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_german_military_command
			add_idea = TUR_german_military_command_0
		}
	}	
}	
recall_GER_TUR_military_mission_effect = {
 	clr_global_flag = GER_TUR_military_mission
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_german_military_command_0 }
		remove_ideas = TUR_german_military_command_0
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_german_military_command }
		remove_ideas = TUR_german_military_command
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_german_military_command_2 }
		remove_ideas = TUR_german_military_command_2
	}
	custom_effect_tooltip = escape_line
	every_character = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_character = GER_colmar_von_der_goltz
				is_character = GER_otto_liman_von_sanders
				is_character = GER_fritz_bronsart_von_schellendorf
				is_character = GER_kress_von_kressenstein
				is_character = GER_wilhelm_souchon
				is_character = GER_guido_von_usedom
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_character = GER_colmar_von_der_goltz
			}
			set_character_name = GER_colmar_von_der_goltz
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_character = GER_otto_liman_von_sanders }
			set_portraits = {
				army = {
					large="gfx/leaders/GER/GER_liman_von_sanders.png"
					small="gfx/interface/ideas/GER/idea_GER_liman_von_sanders.png"
				}
			}
		}
		set_nationality = GER
		hidden_effect = { demote_leader = yes }
	}
}
